<script>

	$(function(){
		sigin_flag = 'modalSigninSignup';
		sigup_flag = 'modalSigninSignup';
	});
	
	function login_register_flag(flag){
		if(flag == 'signin'){
			$('#register_div').hide();
			$('#signin_div').show();
		}else{
			$('#register_div').show();
			$('#signin_div').hide();
			sigup_flag = 'modalSigninSignup';
		}
	}
</script>

        var setTooltip = function (btn, message) {
            btn.tooltip('hide')
                .attr('data-original-title', message)
                .tooltip('show');

        var hideTooltip = function(btn) {
            setTimeout(function () {

          $(document).on('submit', '#jobAlertForm', function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var form_data = $('#jobAlertForm').serialize()+'&rzTkn='+rzTkn;
            $.ajax({
                url: ajax_url + "Job/jobSaveAlert",
                type: 'POST',
                dataType: 'json',
                data: form_data,
            })
                .done(function (res) {
                     $('.success-case').addClass('d-none');
                     $('.invalid-case').addClass('d-none');
                     
                 
                    
                   
                  if(res.code == 200){
                      $('.success-case').removeClass('d-none');
                      $('#success-msg').html(res.message);
                      
                       var myInterval= setInterval(function(){
                       $('#jobalerts').modal('hide');
                     },1000);
                     
                      setTimeout(function(){
                          clearInterval(myInterval);
                      },1100);
                  }
                  else {
                       $('.invalid-case').removeClass('d-none');
                       $('#error-msg').html(res.message);
                  }
                  
                  
                   
                });
        });

            $.ajax({
                url: site_url + 'job/applyJobStep1',
                type: 'POST',
                data: data
            }).always(function (res) {
                if(typeof res == 'object') {
                    $("#applyjob").modal('toggle');
                    if (res.applyAction != 0) {
                        window.location = res.jobUrl;
                        //window.open(res.jobUrl, '_blank');
                    }
                } else {
                    if (res == '0') {
                        $("#load_content").html('Job Detail not found');
                        $("body").addClass("modal-open");
                    } else if (res == '40') {
                        $("#applyjob").modal('toggle');
                        $('#register-signin-modal').modal();
                        return;
                    } else {
                        $("#load_content").html(res);
                        $("body").addClass("modal-open");
                        jobApplyStep1Validation();
                        ApplyJobQuestionsForm();
                    }
                }
                $("#applyLoader").addClass('hide d-none');
            });
            
        }
        $('#register-signin-modal').on('hide.bs.modal', function (e) {
            //loginActType = 0;
            //alert('resetted');
        });
        $(document).on('click', function (e) {
            clickedClass = '';
            if(e.target.getAttribute('class') !== undefined) {
                var clickedClass= e.target.getAttribute('class');
                if(clickedClass !== null && clickedClass !== undefined) {
                    if (clickedClass.indexOf('-R') >= 0) {

                    } else {
                        if (isOpenedSuggestion) {
                            if (window.gReact.jobSuggestionsRender !== undefined)
                                window.gReact.jobSuggestionsRender({});
                            isOpenedSuggestion = false;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            //alert(searchedqry);
        });
        function jobSearch(data) {
            window.gReact.jobSearch(data);
        }

        }
